def audit_files():
    os.makedirs(AUDIT_DIR, exist_ok=True)
    with open(AUDIT_LOG, 'a') as log:
        log.write(f"\n\n<0001f9fe> gTek Master Audit Log: {datetime.datetime.now()}\n")
        for root, _, files in os.walk(EXTRACT_DIR):
            for f in files:
                path = os.path.join(root, f)
                size = os.path.getsize(path)
                sha = hashlib.sha256(open(path, 'rb').read()).hexdigest()
                created = datetime.datetime.fromtimestamp(os.path.getctime(path)).isoformat()
                log.write(f"{path} | {size} bytes | SHA-256: {sha} | Created: {created}\n")
                organize_file(path)
